           Ls*Lt*Sin[Tbl]*Sin[Tmr] + 2*Dxml*Dybl*Dymr*g^2*Lt^2*Sin[Tml]*
           Sin[Tmr] - Dxbl*Dyml*Dymr*g^2*Lt^2*Sin[Tml]*Sin[Tmr]) + 
        Dybr*(g*(Ls*Sin[Tbl] + Lt*Sin[Tml])*(Dxml*Dybl*Dymr*g*Lt*Cos[Tmr] - 
            Dxbl*Dyml*Dymr*g*Lt*Cos[Tmr] - Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*g*Lt*Sin[Tml] + 
            Dxbl*Dxmr*Dyml*g*Lt*Sin[Tml] - Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*g*Lt*Sin[Tmr] + 
            Dxbl*Dxmr*Dyml*g*Lt*Sin[Tmr]) + 
          Dybl*(g*(Ls*Sin[Tbl] + Lt*Sin[Tml])*(-(Dxmr*Dyml*g*Lt*Cos[Tmr]) + 
              Dxml*Dymr*g*Lt*Cos[Tmr] - Dxml*Dxmr*g*Lt*Sin[Tmr]) + 
            g*Lt*Cos[Tml]*(Dxmr*Dyml*g*Lt*Sin[Tml] - Dxml*Dymr*g*Lt*Sin[
                Tml] + Dxmr*Dyml*g*Lt*Sin[Tmr]))))))/
    (g*Ls*Sin[Tbl]*(3*Dxml*Dybl*Dybr*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tml]*
        Cos[Tmr] - 4*Dxbl*Dybr*Dyml*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tml]*
        Cos[Tmr] - 2*Dxbl*Dxmr*Dybr*Dyml*g^3*Ls^2*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tmr]*
        Sin[Tbl] + 3*Dxbl*Dxml*Dybr*Dymr*g^3*Ls^2*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tmr]*
        Sin[Tbl] + Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*Dybr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tml]*Cos[Tmr]*
        Sin[Tbr] - 2*Dxbl*Dxmr*Dybr*Dyml*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tml]*Cos[Tmr]*
        Sin[Tbr] - 4*Dxbr*Dxml*Dybl*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tml]*Cos[Tmr]*
        Sin[Tbr] + 6*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dyml*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tml]*Cos[Tmr]*
        Sin[Tbr] + Dxbl*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybr*g^3*Ls^2*Lt*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbl]*
        Sin[Tbr] + 2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^3*Ls^2*Lt*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbl]*
        Sin[Tbr] - 4*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^3*Ls^2*Lt*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbl]*
        Sin[Tbr] - 2*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*Dybr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tml]*
        Sin[Tml] + 4*Dxbl*Dxmr*Dybr*Dyml*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tml]*
        Sin[Tml] - 2*Dxbl*Dxml*Dybr*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tml]*
        Sin[Tml] - 2*Dxbl*Dxmr*Dybr*Dyml*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tmr]*
        Sin[Tml] + 3*Dxbl*Dxml*Dybr*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tmr]*
        Sin[Tml] + 2*Dxbr*Dxml*Dybl*Dymr*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tml]*Cos[Tmr]*
        Sin[Tml] - 3*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dyml*Dymr*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tml]*Cos[Tmr]*
        Sin[Tml] - Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbl]*
        Sin[Tml] + 2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbl]*
        Sin[Tml] + 2*Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tbr]*
        Sin[Tml] - 4*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tbr]*
        Sin[Tml] + 2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tbr]*
        Sin[Tml] + Dxbl*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbr]*
        Sin[Tml] + 2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbr]*
        Sin[Tml] - 4*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbr]*
        Sin[Tml] - Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tml]^2 + 
       2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tml]^2 - 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tml]^2 - 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tml]^2 + 
       2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tml]^2 - 
       2*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*Dybr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] + 
       4*Dxbl*Dxmr*Dybr*Dyml*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] + 
       Dxbr*Dxml*Dybl*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] - 
       2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dyml*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] - 
       2*Dxbr*Dxml*Dybl*Dymr*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tml]*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tmr] + 
       3*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dyml*Dymr*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tml]*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tmr] - 
       2*Dxbl*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybr*g^3*Ls^2*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tbl]*Sin[Tmr] + 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^3*Ls^2*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tbl]*Sin[Tmr] + 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbl]*Sin[Tmr] - 
       2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbl]*Sin[Tmr] + 
       Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tbr]*Sin[Tmr] - 
       2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tbr]*Sin[Tmr] + 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*g^3*Ls^2*Lt*Sin[Tbl]*Sin[Tbr]*Sin[Tmr] - 
       2*Dxbl*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] + 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] + 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] + 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] - 
       2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] - 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Sin[Tbl]*Sin[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] + 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Sin[Tbr]*Sin[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] - 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*g^3*Lt^3*Sin[Tml]^2*Sin[Tmr] + 
       Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tmr]^2 - 
       2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^3*Lt^3*Cos[Tml]*Sin[Tmr]^2 + 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*g^3*Ls*Lt^2*Sin[Tbl]*Sin[Tmr]^2 + 
       Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*g^3*Lt^3*Sin[Tml]*Sin[Tmr]^2) + 
     g*Ls*Cos[Tbl]*(g*(Ls*Sin[Tbl] + Lt*Sin[Tml])*
        (-3*Dxml*Dybl*Dybr*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tmr] + 
         3*Dxbl*Dybr*Dyml*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tmr] - 
         Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*Dybr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbr] + 
         Dxbl*Dxmr*Dybr*Dyml*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbr] + 
         4*Dxbr*Dxml*Dybl*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbr] - 
         4*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dyml*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbr] + 
         2*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*Dybr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tml] - 
         2*Dxbl*Dxmr*Dybr*Dyml*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tml] - 
         2*Dxbr*Dxml*Dybl*Dymr*g^2*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tml] + 
         2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dyml*Dymr*g^2*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tml] - 
         2*Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*g^2*Ls*Lt*Sin[Tbr]*Sin[Tml] + 
         2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^2*Ls*Lt*Sin[Tbr]*Sin[Tml] + 
         Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*g^2*Lt^2*Sin[Tml]^2 - Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^2*
          Lt^2*Sin[Tml]^2 + 2*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*Dybr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*
          Sin[Tmr] - 2*Dxbl*Dxmr*Dybr*Dyml*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tmr] - 
         Dxbr*Dxml*Dybl*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tmr] + 
         Dxbl*Dxbr*Dyml*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tmr] + 
         2*Dxbr*Dxml*Dybl*Dymr*g^2*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tmr] - 
         2*Dxbl*Dxbr*Dyml*Dymr*g^2*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tmr] - 
         Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*g^2*Ls*Lt*Sin[Tbr]*Sin[Tmr] + 
         Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^2*Ls*Lt*Sin[Tbr]*Sin[Tmr] - 
         Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybl*g^2*Lt^2*Sin[Tmr]^2 + Dxbl*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^2*
          Lt^2*Sin[Tmr]^2) - Dybl*(g*(Ls*Sin[Tbl] + Lt*Sin[Tml])*
          (-2*Dxmr*Dybr*Dyml*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tmr] + 
           3*Dxml*Dybr*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tmr] + Dxml*Dxmr*Dybr*g^2*
            Ls*Lt*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbr] + 2*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tmr]*
            Sin[Tbr] - 4*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbr] - 
           Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^2*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tml] + 2*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^2*
            Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tml] - 2*Dxml*Dxmr*Dybr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*
            Sin[Tmr] + Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tmr] + 
           Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^2*Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tmr] - 2*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^2*
            Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tmr] + Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Sin[Tbr]*
            Sin[Tmr] - Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*g^2*Lt^2*Sin[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] + 
           Dxbr*Dxml*Dxmr*g^2*Lt^2*Sin[Tmr]^2) - g*Lt*Cos[Tml]*
          (Dybr*Dyml*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Cos[Tmr] + Dxmr*Dybr*Dyml*g^2*Ls*
            Lt*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tbr] - 2*Dxbr*Dyml*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tmr]*
            Sin[Tbr] - 2*Dxmr*Dybr*Dyml*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tml] + 
           2*Dxml*Dybr*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tml] + Dxbr*Dyml*Dymr*g^2*
            Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tml] + 2*Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^2*Ls*Lt*Sin[Tbr]*
            Sin[Tml] - 2*Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Sin[Tbr]*Sin[Tml] - 
           Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^2*Lt^2*Sin[Tml]^2 + Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^2*Lt^2*
            Sin[Tml]^2 - 2*Dxmr*Dybr*Dyml*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tmr] + 
           Dxbr*Dyml*Dymr*g^2*Ls*Lt*Cos[Tbr]*Sin[Tmr] - Dxbr*Dyml*Dymr*g^2*
            Lt^2*Cos[Tmr]*Sin[Tmr] + Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^2*Ls*Lt*Sin[Tbr]*
            Sin[Tmr] - Dxbr*Dxml*Dymr*g^2*Lt^2*Sin[Tml]*Sin[Tmr] + 
           Dxbr*Dxmr*Dyml*g^2*Lt^2*Sin[Tmr]^2))))}}
